<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coke.html>coke</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:coke.html>coke</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cokes.html>cokes</a></b>)

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The singular <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> less common than the plural form in Dutch, which may also be used like an uncountable singular. Because of the rarity of the singular <i><a href = vnd.unilang:coke.html>coke</a></i>, some people consider it incorrect.
</p>

<div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/50px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="59" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/75px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/100px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="941" data-file-height="1103" /></div></div>
<div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikispecies" class="extiw" title="w:Wikispecies">Wikispecies</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> information on:
<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><i><b><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Brassica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Brassica">Brassica</a></b></i></div>
</div></div>
<p><span class="interProject"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Brassica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Brassica">Wikispecies <sup></sup></a></span>
From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>cole</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">col</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cawel</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caulis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cabbage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kool.html>kool</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kohl.html>Kohl</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>cole</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coles.html>coles</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cabbage.</li>
<li>Brassica; a plant of the <i>Brassica</i> genus, especially those of <i>Brassica oleracea</i> (rape and coleseed).</li></ol>

***collaborateur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a> (28830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a></i>. The word became the primary label for Nazi collaborators during the Second World War and <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> extremely pejorative ever since.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateurs.html>collaborateurs</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who collaborates or <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> collaborated with the Nazis, fascists or another enemy; traitorous collaborator. <span class="defdate">[from WW II]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">collaborator</span>, one who cooperates on a certain work. <span class="defdate">[19th c. <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> early 1940s]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:collaborateur.html>collaborateur</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenwerkt.html>samenwerkt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:medewerker.html>medewerker</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:bezette.html>bezette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:landen.html>landen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenwerkt.html>samenwerkt</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijke.html>mannelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> collaboratrice</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:collaboratie.html>collaboratie</a> (52186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaboratie.html>collaboratie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaboratie.html>collaboraties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:collaboratie.html>collaboratietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>collaboration</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The term <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a negative connotation. To many people, it means collaboration with the German occupier during the Second World War.

***collier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:collier.html>collier</a> (9356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">colier</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">col</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg/220px-SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg/330px-SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg/440px-SS_%27Wandle%27_%281932%29_on_maiden_voyage.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="453" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SS_Wandle_(1932)" class="extiw" title="w:SS Wandle (1932)">S.S. <i>Wandle</i></a>, a British <a href = vnd.unilang:collier.html>collier</a>, arriving on her maiden voyage at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pool_of_London" class="extiw" title="w:Pool of London">Pool of London</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/London" class="extiw" title="w:London">London</a>, England, UK</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:collier.html>collier</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:colliers.html>colliers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person in the business or occupation of producing (digging or mining) coal or making charcoal or in its transporting or commerce.
<ul><li><b>1957</b>, H.<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Schubert, <i>History of the British Iron and Steel Industry</i>, p. 224.
<dl><dd>For this reason, the <a href = vnd.unilang:collier.html>collier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> constant care to keep the covering of earth in good order.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A vessel carrying a bulk cargo of coal.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sailor on such a vessel.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> used by the traveller community</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A non-traveller.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:colliers.html>Colliers</a> Wood</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">colliery</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:collier.html>collier</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***combinatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:combinatie.html>combinatie</a> (4214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">combination</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">combination</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">combinatio</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:combineren.html>combineren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:combinatie.html>combinatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:combinaties.html>combinaties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:combinatie.html>combinatietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>combination
<ol><li>the act, process or outcome of combining</li>
<li>a set-up of a <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a> and one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:trailers.html>trailers</a></li>
<li>a series of <a href = vnd.unilang:moves.html>moves</a> in chess</li>
<li>a series of <a href = vnd.unilang:moves.html>moves</a> in martial <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a></li></ol></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">commerce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commercium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">commerce, trade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">com-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">merx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good, wares, merchandise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:commissaris.html>commissaris</a> (2222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:commissaris.html>commissaris</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:commissarissen.html>commissarissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:commissaris.html>commissarisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***commissie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:commissie.html>commissie</a> (3716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">commission</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commissio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sending together; commission</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from prefix <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">com-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, + noun of action <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sending</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mittō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, + noun of action suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-io</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:commotie.html>commotie</a> (24606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:commotie.html>commotie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">commocion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commōtiō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commōtus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commoveō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">commotion</span> (agitation).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstond.html>ontstond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nogal.html>nogal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a><i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:commotie.html>commotie</a></b> </i><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:atlete.html>atlete</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gediskwalificeerd.html>gediskwalificeerd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> considerable <b>commotion</b> when the athlete <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> disqualified.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">communicacie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">communicacion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commūnicātiōnem</i>, accusative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commūnicātiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">imparting, communicating</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commūnicō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I share, I impart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:communiceren.html>communiceren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kommunismus</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>communism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collectivist socialism, ideology</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Sovjetblok <a href = vnd.unilang:verloor.html>verloor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>Koude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>Oorlog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:westers.html>Westers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kapitalisme.html>kapitalisme</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>Muur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Soviet block's <b>Communism</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> the Cold War against Western capitalism when the Wall <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>communism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">classless and stateless international socialist order</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Marx <a href = vnd.unilang:voorspelde.html>voorspelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> eindstadium <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwikkeling.html>ontwikkeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereldorde.html>wereldorde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Marx predicted that <b>communism</b> would be the final stage of the development of the world order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any collectivism

***compenseren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:compenseren.html>compenseren</a> (16288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:compenseren.html>compenseren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">compenser</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compenseren.html>compenseren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to compensate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compensatie.html>compensatie</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
